              <a id="23974" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23976" href="univalent-combinatorics.orientations-complete-undirected-graph.html#23684" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="23977" class="Symbol">)))))</a> <a id="23983" class="Symbol">→</a>
